I found the issue! Look at lines 305-310:\n\n```python\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_515_3].copy_add_setting(\n    _Setting('increase_text_contrast', 'IncreaseTextContrast', _INT_BOOLS),\n)\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_64] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63].copy_replace_setting(\n    'threshold.text', 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold',\n)\n```\n\nIn Qt 6.4, they're trying to replace the setting name from 'threshold.text' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. However, looking at the `copy_replace_setting` method on lines 251-263:\n\n```python\ndef copy_replace_setting(self, option: str, chromium_key: str) -> '_Definition':\n    \"\"\"Get a new _Definition object with `old` replaced by `new`.\n\n    If `old` is not in the settings list, return the old _Definition object.\n    \"\"\"\n    new = copy.deepcopy(self)\n\n    for setting in new._settings:  # pylint: disable=protected-access\n        if setting.option == option:\n            setting.chromium_key = chromium_key\n            return new\n\n    raise ValueError(f\"Setting {option} not found in {self}\")\n```\n\nThis method takes an `option` (like 'threshold.text') and a `chromium_key` (like 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'). But when you look at the call:\n\n```python\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_64] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63].copy_replace_setting(\n    'threshold.text', 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold',\n)\n```\n\nThe problem is that the `chromium_key` parameter should include the full key including the prefix. \n\nLooking at line 233, the prefix gets added when the setting is used:\n\n```python\nyield switch, setting.with_prefix(self.prefix)\n```\n\nSo when we replace the chromium_key to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', and the prefix is '' (empty), the result should be 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. But the actual issue is in the definition itself—qt_63 has `_Setting('threshold.text', 'TextBrightnessThreshold')`, and when the prefix gets applied (which is '' for qt_515_3 and qt_63), the chromium_key doesn't match what Qt 6.4 expects.\n\nWhen we call `copy_replace_setting('threshold.text', 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold')`, we're updating the chromium_key correctly. The comments in the file (lines 91-99) explain that Qt 6.4 renamed TextBrightnessThreshold to ForegroundBrightnessThreshold as part of a change to the darkmode color classifier, with references to the specific Chromium review commits that made this change.","signature":"EvAWCkYICxgCKkCqABEntCWIqqLvD31awJZTtDYMf4uN1ZCBBmnoccCWEEtXtQGRYYw+bzD6d4RP5kioBabqn5QRv4uRVvZCXkX5EgwXRswnQCogRginZR0aDMOJ3hvz/vp8Zgn8NSIwx7Piitp8LhzhkJhAKkDle5tYEPUPEq0iVw9Ys05jgWpMYkjkPB9BOCuGautjvQmSKtcVfFIRMoF4LgoQhFMVaEpTxK88b48hP9Ppf79ZgALxpMaBU2zKyxV7bUxUfgCyQTi2od7bKalgW80WGdbxrJYTzC0wU8A5ro4Oag3MAR96Mk7odGjpp5tS958epXHjyr7w5nxA069oaVfDJG+Soal+cafWeEsDkEN2jlHfKIGAayy063Rwta9hFLZGdt5l5zg90MGWUNV1DPyHuGP5GP0j3IiM9atW/8HRyTfjzXtQAhFof90SEevLzBmem8qZjRgX07lhG276iq0Y2hJQw7nwcqwE0AkUo2946BN+fVU1hfxfpdUw6b1EwDfR6vgDMAm/LXt6Kndn+Wez5w9L2Y3m7T42GAtSiiuh4+15twEcsYxknMsTt8y83Q4vdufI6+1cmSuFEwJy6YzpMv13B3oN/fEL8FN5zz0D4Kf7/EYTnnVOJyjfxyP+Hq2dCBhV1fqyETs8a1HjEQ2T15MkhH5tMtZisi/XaXNw2oV4YdoI9/pdiwTtHGbhpKFfMdKcPcJ7lzhjCuLF8hdm/LsjxhoqQhupZ8qd/Hjd0jMRxQEQfXVs6FoaHedCQEAENWdoJM8S4GZVj7bAeJ4SMtnYpP01IiLbnhMpQF2g+DV+CNOpmlkQgMgUWaMw61BTpuiUM6mylZ6Dzb9klzkbB7O+Cou9coCxFll5QtjNNg0A17d71Dj/K6gmUB2294dEQULXwdwO2e9fD4fVCS8GDhaOLiwBIjUUqMpZzByhpBZpxJbnODpA9HKAtEaK/QxhC+QoysZnaCRJP3fl3As4Q+XA1CGNMPn8Onn5EdTX60pXtbgBBb8cf8TZpIxeJe4j0uHrxC61mMN6uM+rx1qtvV9CFSayhVFs/vbL9ZRFQ/aSPgdkQlBp8IRcYzX9cbknCcrYdO1zuGSuSt99GeOsnNWSkNDrS16YvxGWNdEVgDOlwc+IDUYgJkvyVpV0OCmus2wIT6p1BO28wRrYZfQiq4BRup0PUnAT6b85KFbFeMrK4kCIkg1Fu7vY0Mhs8hPiKmJ0Ax3oaSgdAk401y0kW0iJ7Diok5Ps2q0tpv1yi93OSPSdaNou1mvHs5M/lx6rT0gl9KTlY5vu5saqcF7BnzJ+fJODdwIpwoElZOhDGgRwXCVTI/0YaUhrhAihnmbNyTmyzVUlhLqtlNob/JNV3URxG6f9c4Ndyuc6KunvqjTV4RzCUkFxYrBmerRK4WrZhvuMVIOwS82H3DcgqdWiIy2TxIQy8TzFckAcFyuuZ6x0Q5ItbUfviIzmqlLegSf3YeL6d0eH/NOZlnDw+d7tzrgYWcbIzSxFHTfzehQq5gcvEh03sIRhzFpcmpTvoKjQcWnHxn03U/2sUpLGFe3U5MaC9Mr4Z6xpDq7YzfIp9Em4Y1c+YR12GextHR3ZCjA7t2kNW3+U6p7yzkFEKFcp7bM9CnoOm0TS4G+puaPzlc/JHXeMBWUKPU8jkLbbeCLc3amMX8FBqyNGY3rhoIakuRnfS3e26+pCN8kNKQPwdlDMZrdIsuC1oRETdeI8ujZOKe+Nxwo9sVYBRd4iHkZApHfraqnK6lPBXf0Tf2S7YzBDh3WLO1GenpohbraLDsNhMbQauApsxkk+aqN95PSokS3f6u1FF26KSsP6IeEUA5I873yN+E8G/jznhYwkG2EgtAMFFdRTVfY8jNJW7Mfh6kHRNu9SpB7DBT9P18njc01zhp0fniaKPs2l2FzLmp8Hh78hpY86pKE0//7maYeoFD7mD1DgyjeQTwzrkij8q57mtoV7ik If this works as intended, the method returns a new definition with the updated setting rather than raising an exception.\n\nBut the actual issue isn't a crash—it's that the setting gets ignored entirely when running Qt 6.4. The `settings()` function retrieves the variant and builds the configuration, but somewhere in that process the threshold value isn't being applied to dark mode rendering.\n\nLooking at how the code fetches each setting: it gets the variant definition, then iterates through the prefixed settings to pull the config value for each option. The problem might be in how `prefixed_settings()` prepares or returns those settings, or perhaps the variant definition itself is missing or misconfigured for Qt 6.4. For Qt 6.4, the prefix remains empty, so the chromium_key resolves to just 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. This checks out so far. But looking more closely at the definitions, Qt 6.3 adds 'IncreaseTextContrast' as a new setting, while Qt 6.4 replaces the 'threshold.text' setting with 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. The issue might be in how this replacement is being handled or what the original setting looked like before the replacement. _Definition object with a replaced setting. If the option isn't found in the settings list, it returns the original _Definition object unchanged.\n\nThe method uses `copy.deepcopy(self)` to create a complete deep copy, then iterates through the settings to find and modify the matching chromium_key. So Qt 6.3 starts as a shallow copy of Qt 5.15.3 with an added setting in the tuple, while Qt 6.4 is a deep copy of Qt 6.3 where one setting's chromium_key gets updated. This layering of shallow and deep copies should work correctly without unintended mutations.\n\nBut the bug report claims the setting has no effect on Qt 6.4. Looking at the Chromium changes around that version, there's a rename from TextBrightnessThreshold to ForegroundBrightnessThreshold, plus a classifier rename. The issue might not be a simple rename—Chromium could have altered the setting's actual behavior or how it's
